```
<output>For every eight coffees purchased, you should add the cost of one free coffee to the total bill, but instead, you're adding the cost of nine coffees. Try changing `bill += bill + 8 * pricePerCoffee` to `bill += 8 * pricePerCoffee`. Also, consider handling edge cases like zero or negative values for `numberOfCoffees` and `pricePerCoffee`, which might not be valid inputs.</output>
```

```
You are using floor division (//) which discards the remainder and returns the quotient as an integer, effectively ignoring the free coffee. Instead, use the division operator (/) to get a floating-point result.</output>
```
